         <div class="details-section description simple contains-text-link">
          <div class="details-section-contents show-more-container" data-show-use-buffer="true">
           <h1 class="heading">
            Description
           </h1>
           <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description">
            <div class="id-app-orig-desc">
             Mini word, puzzle and trivia games with daily prizes!
             <br/>
             <br/>
             <p>
              Like Family Feud, Two Tribes or Apples to Apples? You'll love The Pryz Manor! Each room in The Pryz Manor hosts a fun prediction, word, image or trivia game with real prizes. Enter the kitchen to predict which prizes are the most popular, and win your favorite. Put your trivia knowledge, deduction skills and memory to the test in Name Dropper, our lightning fast word game.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              Send hints, clues and power-ups to help your partner guess a trivia topic from pop culture, sports, movies, TV or music. The more words you guess, the more prizes you can win!
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </p>
             <p>
              <b>
               Highlights:
              </b>
              <br/>
               Play 4 free games
              <br/>
               Compete for daily prizes
              <br/>
               Challenge your friends and family
              <br/>
               Test your trivia knowledge
              <br/>
               Unlock new prizes and power-ups
              <br/>
               Send free hints and power-ups
              <br/>
               Trade in your bloons for prizes
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </p>
             <p>
              Download now for free to start winning prizes!
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </p>
             <p>
              ...don't just take our word for it. Check out our player reviews:
              <br/>
              James- 5/5 'Addictive: download at your own risk!'
              <br/>
              Suzette- 5/5 'Best game out there right now.'
              <br/>
              Tamara- 5/5 'Love the games and the prizes.'
              <br/>
              Mike- 5/5 'Completely addictive cross between taboo and who wants to be a millionaire'
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </p>
             <p>
              ***The Pryz Manor is still under construction. If you come across any issues, please email
              <a href="mailto:support@thepryzmanor.com">
               support@thepryzmanor.com
              </a>
              so we can fix them***
              <br/>
              <br/>
             </p>
             <p>
              ***********
             </p>
             <p>
              <b>
               About Upfront Analytics
              </b>
              <br/>
              Upfront Analytics is a market intelligence company based in Dublin, Ireland. Our games are different from most mobile games in that we use game responses to try and understand players opinions and behaviors. We keep your personal responses strictly confidential and generate market intelligence only from the aggregate responses of many players. Check out our privacy policy to learn more.
             </p>
             <p>
              ***********
             </p>
             <p>
              Suggestions?
              <br/>
              Email:
              <a href="mailto:suggestions@thepryzmanor.com">
               suggestions@thepryzmanor.com
              </a>
              <br/>
              Twitter: @thepryzmanor
             </p>
             <p>
              Support requests?
              <br/>
              Email:
              <a href="mailto:support@thepryzmanor.com">

              </a>
              <br/>
              Twitter: @tpmsupport
             </p>

              Alternative titles: the prize manor, prize manor, pryz manor
             </p>
